  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">"Petite Tueuse"? Considering the name of her sword, the best translation is probably "Little Slayer" (tueuse is the feminine form of tueur = murderer,<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">"Petite Tueuse"? Considering the name of her sword, the best translation is probably "Little Slayer" (tueuse is the feminine form of tueur = murderer, killer, slaughterer).<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1443880831" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer940627201606438327"><b>
  <u>The Top 8 Reasons why you should drop everything you're doing and grab the Kate Daniels series ASAP</u>
</b><br/>(focusing on <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4345498.Magic_Strikes__Kate_Daniels___3_' title='Magic Strikes (Kate Daniels, #3) by Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Magic Strikes</a>)<br/><br/><u>1. The huge variety of mythology</u>: celtic, greek, and now norse and <b>hindu</b>. Honestly, every supernatural creature you've ever heard will make an appearance, preferably soaked in blood and other substances I dare not name, and will deliver you extraordinary threats, unique bloodbath and eventually it will be killed in the most badass way.<br/><br/><u>2. The Midnight Games. </u>An undergr</span>
  <span id="freeText940627201606438327" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>The Top 8 Reasons why you should drop everything you're doing and grab the Kate Daniels series ASAP</u>
</b><br>(focusing on <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4345498.Magic_Strikes__Kate_Daniels___3_" title="Magic Strikes (Kate Daniels, #3) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a>)<br><br><u>1. The huge variety of mythology</u>: celtic, greek, and now norse and <b>hindu</b>. Honestly, every supernatural creature you've ever heard will make an appearance, preferably soaked in blood and other substances I dare not name, and will deliver you extraordinary threats, unique bloodbath and eventually it will be killed in the most badass way.<br><br><u>2. The Midnight Games. </u>An underground gladiatorial tournament with a magic jewel as a price. We're talking about a massacre of epic proportions that would make George Martin weep with pride. And the participants? Minotaurs, golems, mages and of course our Valiant Knights of the Fur. Prepare for major ass kicking.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427752537ra/14317338.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>3. Kate Daniels.</u><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I gave him a smile. I was aiming for sweet, but he turned a shade paler and scooted a bit farther from me. Note to self: work more on sweet and less on psycho-killer.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404544884ra/10255259.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><u>4. The action.</u> I will admit that while reading the first chapters I thought <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4345498.Magic_Strikes__Kate_Daniels___3_" title="Magic Strikes (Kate Daniels, #3) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a> would be a 4 stars read, they seemed pretty lame compared to the incredible plotline of the second book. But oh boy I was so wrong! Once the plot thickened with rogue shapeshifters and the kill-or-be-killed tournament, <b>I.couldn't.stop.reading.</b> This series keeps getting better and I have a feeling that sky is the limit!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438149411ra/15669999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>5. The side characters.</u> Whether they're <i>sexual deviants</i> or uptight cats or pretty werewolves or devastatingly handsome sex addicts, they're a great addition to the story, with their wit and loyalty and friendship.<br><br><u>6. Curran, the Beast Lord of Atlanta, the Leader of the Pack, and Asshole Supreme.</u><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“...you expect me to fall on my back with my legs spread."<br>"Not necessarily. ... You can fall on your hands and knees if you prefer. Or against the wall. Or on the kitchen counter. I suppose I might let you be on top, if you make it worth my while.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>You get the picture.<br><br><u>7. The romance.</u><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Kiss me and I'll kill you,”I warned.<br>“It might be worth it,”he said softly.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The will-or-won't-they status keeps going, and it can be frustrating as hell, but it's the right course. Besides the <b>sizzling tension</b> and their fights, in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4345498.Magic_Strikes__Kate_Daniels___3_" title="Magic Strikes (Kate Daniels, #3) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a> we saw how much Curran and Kate care for each other, that despite their differences there is something strong brewing between them, something more than raw attraction. <b>They're falling in love.</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He caressed my cheek.<br>"You came for me," I whispered.<br>"Always," he told me.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>8. The.hot.tub.scene.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/502032.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You're welcome.<br>Love,<br>Katerina</span>
  <a data-text-id="940627201606438327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText17402680902048720973" style="display:none">🐈 <b>The Adventures Of A Brave Little Kitty Buddy Rerererereread</b> (TAOABLKBR™) with the IA Addicts 🐈<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this particular rererererereread is:</u>
</b> tinmen on steroids and overgrown logs are no match for <b>Kate Daniels, sausage expert extraordinaire</b>. Ha. And now let's dance and stuff. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1555355061ra/27367346.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>P.S.</b> Nonchalance is the <b>best camouflage for drooling</b>. Just so you know.<br><br>👋 <b>Until next time and stuff</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>December 2017</b>]<br><br>⚔ <b>
  <u>The Grand IAA™ KD Buddy Rerererereread Extravaganza</u>
</b> (GIAAKDBRE™), aka the <s>yellow brick</s> road to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17333180.Magic_Triumphs__Kate_Daniels___10_" title="Magic Triumphs (Kate Daniels, #10) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Triumphs</a> ⚔<br><br><i><b>Presenting Episode 3</b>, or How Kate Daniels Learned not all Cats Hate <s>Water</s> Hot Tubs</i>.<br><br>» <b>
  <u>And the moral of this particular rererereread is:</u>
</b> <b>TWT-IHFB</b> is the best bloody shrimping acronym in the history of <b>bloody shrimping acronyms</b>. Trust me on that one, I practically invented the concept. Of bloody shrimping acronyms, I mean. <b>Not of TWT-IHFBs</b>. I wish I had, though. Because it's, you know, the best acronym in the history of <b>bloody shrimping acronyms</b> and stuff.<br><br>» <b>
  <u>And the other moral of this particular rererereread is:</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1512847110i/24638639.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>And who doesn't love</b> <s>aggravating cats</s> <s>sneaky kitties</s> <s>the universe exploding</s> <s>Curran</s> <b>trouble</b>?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>June 2016</b>]<br><br>❣ <b>KD is the Cure to All of Life's Problems Buddy Read</b> (KDitCtAoLPBR™) with my dear wife <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4255477-angela" rel="nofollow noopener">Ange</a>, and the poor <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">IAA</a> souls who have fallen into our deathly <b>KD Surprise Reread Trap</b> (KSRT™).<br><br>✎ <b>Original rating</b>: 5 stars<br>✎ <b>Rating after xxxxxx rereads</b>: boom. The universe exploded. This book is so <b>BLOODY AWESOME</b>, it's bloody unratable.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465573115ra/19375586.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>See? Even my dog decided to do a crazy dance to celebrate the total, utter and complete awesomeness that is this book.</i><br><br>» <b>And the moral</b> of this particular rererereread is: Midnight Games + hot tubs + the Scarlet Star + a flying palace = it doesn't get much better than this. <b>Bye now</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>Original review</b>]<br><br><i>☆☆☆ Post-Shift Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br><b>Just Another Day in the Life of Kate Daniels</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422176678i/13467151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>►<b>8.00 a.m.:</b> roll out of bed after getting 2 hours of sleep. Realize you're hungry. Open the fridge to get some of that leftover apple pie. <b>The plate is empty.</b> Strange.<br>► <b>8.30 a.m.:</b> rescue your teenage werewolf sidekick from Saiman. Watch Saiman change form and <b>throw up in your mouth</b> a little.<br>► <b>9.00 a.m.:</b> find out His Furriness became Beast Lord at the tender age of 15 after chopping Andorf's head off. <b>This is going to be a long day.</b><br>► <b>9.30 a.m.:</b> your best friend tells you she doesn't want to be Raphael's TWT-IHFB. <b>Oh boy.</b><br>► <b>10.00 a.m.:</b> have a conversation with His Fussiness about <b>kissing his ass</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422183078i/13468319.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>10.30 a.m.:</b> hand Saiman a needle so he can <b>pop his head with it</b>. It's obscuring your view of the room.<br>► <b>11.00 a.m.:</b> listen to Jim telling you about a <b>weredingo</b>. Consider yourself lucky he didn't steal your baby.<br>► <b>11.30 a.m.:</b> try to smile. Aim for sweet. End up looking like a <b>psycho-killer</b>.<br>► <b>12.00 a.m.:</b> listen to a lecture about the different shapeshifter courtship customs. Aunt B. A cat on the ceiling. A fan. Mist. <b>That's boudas for you</b>.<br>► <b>12.30 a.m.:</b> go sightseeing with Jim. Visit a jungle and a flying palace. Play with the locals. <b>Chop a few arms off</b>. Things are looking up.<br>► <b>1.00 p.m.:</b> tell His Furriness he's a deadly psychopath with a god complex. Then tell him you're <b>having rough sex with Jim</b>. Bad idea.<br>► <b>1.30 p.m.:</b> temporary insanity. Oh. My. God. <b>The Universe just exploded</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422182147ra/13468218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>2.00 p.m.:</b> explain to your furry friends why you want Cesare's head. Then proceed to explain how you plan to <b>resurrect it and make it relive its death</b> over and over again. Did you just say all that out loud? Yep. You did.<br>► <b>2.30 p.m.:</b> the Beast Lord asks you <b>why you always attract creeps</b>. Ha! He walked right into that one, yes, he did.<br>► <b>3.00 p.m.:</b> Andrea says M-A-T-E. <b>You curse</b>. Then consider strangling her a little.<br>► <b>3.30 p.m.:</b> fight in the arena. Jim tells you to be sloppy. <b>You try</b>.<br>► <b>4.00 p.m.:</b> have a conversation about sausages with your furry friends. <i>
  <b>Die, die, die, die.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422181927ra/13468163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>4.30 p.m.:</b> Raphael hands you a fan in case you get hot. Curran doesn't think you need it. <b>This cat's such a bore</b>.<br>► <b>5.00 p.m.:</b> remember the good old days with daddy Voron back when you were thirteen. <b>Sightseeing in South America</b>. Visiting arenas. Slaughtering things a bit.<br>► <b>5.30 p.m.:</b> another fight in the arena. Blade-sprouting silver golem ✓ Troll (aka the overgrown log) ✓ Ancient vampire ✓ Enjoy seeing them die ✓ <b>This is so much fun</b>.<br>► <b>6.00 p.m.:</b> take a relaxing bath in a hot tub. <b>Try to pretend the Beast Lord isn't in there with you</b>. Oh. My. God. The Universe just exploded again.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422182147ra/13468218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>6.30 p.m.:</b> yet another fight in the arena. <b>Oh, look, it's the Scarlet Star</b>. <i>"Hessaad." Mine. "Ud." Die.</i> Sorry daddy, I think I just broke your sword.<br>► <b>7.00 p.m.:</b> Oh look, it's the flying palace again. <b>Feeling suddenly very tired</b>. It's been a long day.<br>► <b>7.30 p.m.:</b> Lose a little blood. <b>Cut a head off</b>. Feel much better.<br>► <b>8.00 p.m.:</b> find out cats are suicidal morons. <b>Who would have thought?</b><br>► <b>8.30 p.m.:</b> try telling the people in your head to shut up. <b>It doesn't work</b>. Oh look, a cat.<br>► <b>9.00 p.m.:</b> go home. Find someone in your kitchen. <b>Wait. What?</b><br>► <b>9.30 p.m.:</b> read a note reminding you of an upcoming dinner. <b>You're allowed to wear a bra and panties</b>. Oh boy.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422119861i/13458929.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>· <b>Book 1</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156913295" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 2</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1136556683" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 4</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1222662503" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bleeds</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 5</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156907200" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Slays</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 6</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1087380222" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Rises</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 7</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1222671908" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Breaks</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 8</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088122695" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Shifts</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 9</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1388386563" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Binds</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 10</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1767301739" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Triumphs</a> ★★★★</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=vampires-and-werewolves-oh-my">vampires-and-werewolves-oh-my</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=you-go-girl-kickass-heroine">you-go-girl-kickass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=sometimes-fun-beats-profound">sometimes-fun-beats-profound</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=r-rated">r-rated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1208717107" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5560976104805970126">All the stars! I enjoyed the first two books in this Kate Daniels series, but <i>Magic Strikes</i> reached new levels of fun and games (of the gladiator death match variety) and just sheer awesomeness.<br/><br/>Kate Daniels and her werewolf, werehyena, and other shapeshifter friends get mixed up with some shady goings-on in connection with the Midnight Games, an underground organization that puts on illegal, to-the-death cage fights of the magical variety. Kate's young werewolf friend Derek decides to get involv</span>
  <span id="freeText5560976104805970126" style="display:none">All the stars! I enjoyed the first two books in this Kate Daniels series, but <i>Magic Strikes</i> reached new levels of fun and games (of the gladiator death match variety) and just sheer awesomeness.<br><br>Kate Daniels and her werewolf, werehyena, and other shapeshifter friends get mixed up with some shady goings-on in connection with the Midnight Games, an underground organization that puts on illegal, to-the-death cage fights of the magical variety. Kate's young werewolf friend Derek decides to get involved in rescuing a lovely young woman from a particularly vicious group. Saiman has a stake in the Midnight Games, but events get personal for him as well.<br><br>Meanwhile, Julie, Kate's teenage friend/mentee/adoptive daughter, is having trouble adjusting in school, so Kate decides some impressing of Julie's schoolmates in order, which results in one of the most delightful scenes in the book. I reread that scene probably four times. Curran, with his Beast Lord magnificence, is slowly closing in on Kate. (I hypothetically might have read a certain hot tub scene three or four times as well.) I also LOVE a legal throwdown Kate does when Jim, the Pack's chief of security, tries to stonewall her.<blockquote>"James Damael Shrapshire, in your capacity as the Pack's chief security officer, you have permitted Pack members under your command to deliberately injure an employee of the Order. At least three individuals involved in the assault word the shapeshifter warrior form. Under the Georgia code, a shapeshifter in a warrior form is equivalent to being armed with a deadly weapon. Therefore, your actions fall under O.C.G.A. Section 16-5-21(c), aggravated assault on a peace officer engaged in the performance of her duties, which is punishable by mandatory imprisonment of no less than five and no more than twenty years. A formal complaint will be filed with the Order within twenty-four hours. I advise you to seek the assistance of counsel." <br><br>Jim stared at me. The hardness drained from his eyes, and in their depths I saw astonishment.</blockquote>Legal prowess FTW!<br><br>Characters make mistakes, but they're not idiotic mistakes where you want to slap them upside the head and/or hurl the book against the wall. <i>Magic Strikes</i> weaves in another culture's mythology again, Hindu in this case (who knew about Rakshasas and vimanas before reading this book? Not I). And we start getting some real answers to some of the mysteries about Kate's background and parents that I've wondered about since early in book #1. Total win!<br><br>I was originally thinking 4 stars for this book, but then I realized a couple of things: First, I keep going back to the book to reread my favorite scenes. Also, I decided it's not fair to compare this book to <i>Pride and Prejudice</i> or other classic or literary masterpieces. This is urban fantasy. It's meant to be smart (and smartass), enjoyable, fantastical, and sexy. <i>Magic Strikes</i> is all of these things, and I really can't think of a better book in this particular genre. If we're comparing apples to apples, this is like the best UF apple <b>ever</b>.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425070217i/13840729._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><i>Art credit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://strikerv2.deviantart.com/art/Fantasy-Apple-162813008">http://strikerv2.deviantart.com/art/F...</a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5560976104805970126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6957165305072063329">Did you guys watch American Gladiators when you were kids? I just looked it up on IMDB, and the show's first run was from 1989-1997.<-----eight years is a LONG time. <br/><br/>Long enough for most of you to have watched it at some point during your childhood. B/c really? What's better than ridiculously muscled men (and women) in red, white, and blue spandex with names like Nitro and Laser . . . and MALIBU (Oh yeaaah):<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405868503i/10462940.jpg' width='350' height='261' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>GAWD, I love the 80's. <br/><br/>And Malibu could totally be Curran in the middle of the magic flar</span>
  <span id="freeText6957165305072063329" style="display:none">Did you guys watch American Gladiators when you were kids? I just looked it up on IMDB, and the show's first run was from 1989-1997.&lt;-----eight years is a LONG time. <br><br>Long enough for most of you to have watched it at some point during your childhood. B/c really? What's better than ridiculously muscled men (and women) in red, white, and blue spandex with names like Nitro and Laser . . . and MALIBU (Oh yeaaah):<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405868503i/10462940.jpg" width="350" height="261" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>GAWD, I love the 80's. <br><br>And Malibu could totally be Curran in the middle of the magic flare. I mean, look at that hair. (Don't worry, Curran isn't some gym rat with 80's hair. The magic flare just made it grow REALLY fast. As soon as it was over he hacked it all off, I promise.)<br><br>The point is that b/c of my glorious upbringing, I'm predisposed to like anything gladiator related. I could lie and say that I love it b/c of my extensive studies of western civilization, but really it's b/c of this:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405870200i/10463208.jpg" width="384" height="267" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405868968i/10463041.jpg" width="500" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>#sorrynotsorry<br><br>Right. So, Kate's having the longest day ever, and is just about ready to finally go home when Maxine asks her to look into a report of a Pack death. But when she gets to the site, Jim is all, "I got this," so Kate goes home. <br><br>To her pie. (&lt;-----Ehehehehe)<br><br>And almost immediately gets a call from Saiman. <br><br>Derek broke into his apartment, you see, and would Kate care to come and get him, or should Saiman contact the police to handle it instead?<br><br><i>Of course</i> Kate goes to get Derek, but she has to agree to accompany Saiman to the MIDNIGHT GAMES in return for his silence. Kate and Boy Wonder hit the road, but before they part ways, Derek gives her a note . . . <br><br>For a girl . . . at the MIDNIGHT GAMES. <br><br>I wish we had neural implants that were triggered when you read "MIDNIGHT GAMES." It would echo and sound like one of those small car dealership or furniture warehouse "MIDNIGHT MADNESS SALE" commercials. B/c that would be awesome.<br><br>Anyway, stuff happens, including, but not limited to Kate telling Jim that he can stick his, "I got this," attitude where the sun don't shine, Kate telling Curran that she's running away with Jim, and Curran losing his mind. <br><br>Have I mentioned that this is my FAVORITE book in my FAVORITE series? <br><br>'Cause it is.<br><br>And not just b/c of the MIDNIGHT GAMES (which is, admittedly, significant). MAGIC STRIKES is just one big mass of awesome. In fact, there is so much awesome that it deserves a list:<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[1. The Jim smackdown.<br>2. Raphael and Kate going to pick up Julie.<br>3. HOT TUB.<br>4. Blood spikes in Cesare's head.<br>5. Curran in the loup cage.<br>6. Finding out Doolittle is a HONEY BADGER.<br>7. Finding out Saiman is part LOKI.<br>8. HUGH D'AMBREY.<br><br>And that's just off the top of my head. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>This book is everything that Urban Fantasy is supposed to be. It does not get better than this. If you like UF, and you haven't read this series and this book, your opinion on other series and books in this genre isn't going to carry as much weight with me. If you <i>have</i> read and loved it, your recommendations gain credibility. If I find a new person who loves KATE DANIELS, I friend request them. If you friend request me saying that you love Kate too, I accept. That's how fantastic this series and this book are. The end. <br><br><b>My other reviews for this series:</b><br><br><b>

<div id="review_45913706" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45913706" />
    <a title="Shannon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon"><img alt="Shannon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572638169p2/2016128.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/45913706?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon">Shannon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shannon by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/355739-the-flooze">The Flooze</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=strips">strips</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=gods">gods</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-brown">color-brown</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-purple">color-purple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=sexy-urban-fantasy">sexy-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=2010">2010</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer45913706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4652877282875403984">Alright, alright. I am now fully entrenched in the "I Love the Kate Daniels Series" camp. <b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38619.Magic_Bites__Kate_Daniels___1_' title='Magic Bites (Kate Daniels, #1) by Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Magic Bites</a> was ok, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45911879' rel='nofollow noopener'>Magic Burns</a> was better, and Magic Strikes had me grinning from ear to ear at the last page.</b> I'm desperate now to read the next one to see what happens with Kate and Curran. The tension they've built up is absolutely delicious. THIS is how you create a relationship in a series. I hate authors that think throwing the two characters into bed with each other right away is either realistic, p</span>
  <span id="freeText4652877282875403984" style="display:none">Alright, alright. I am now fully entrenched in the "I Love the Kate Daniels Series" camp. <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38619.Magic_Bites__Kate_Daniels___1_" title="Magic Bites (Kate Daniels, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a> was ok, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45911879" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a> was better, and Magic Strikes had me grinning from ear to ear at the last page.</b> I'm desperate now to read the next one to see what happens with Kate and Curran. The tension they've built up is absolutely delicious. THIS is how you create a relationship in a series. I hate authors that think throwing the two characters into bed with each other right away is either realistic, plausible, or sexy. Most of the time it makes me roll my eyes. I think the first Mona Lisa book by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/11859.Sunny" title="Sunny" rel="nofollow noopener">Sunny</a> had the two main characters jump each others bones within the first 10 pages. Ridiculous and unsatisfying, and it made me think less of her characters and the author for creating it. (I only mention Sunny because I just finished a book by her, trying to giver her a second chance. My advice: don't bother.)<br /><br />Anyway, getting back to Magic Strikes.<br /><br /><i>At the start, Kate is extremely tired and overworked. After one too many jobs she gets a call that a shapeshifter has been murdered. She goes to investigate, already exhausted and craving her bed and some pie she left in the fridge, and finds a bunch of shapeshifters at the scene combing for evidence. Before she can even get close though, a shifter walks up to her and tells her they have it under control. And then Jim, Curran's chief of security as well as her friend and fellow mercenary, drops from the shadows and tells her to leave. He won't let her see the body and he doesn't want her help or interference. She leaves, although the situation nags at her. And rightly so, since the creatures that killed the shifter come after her and her friends, and threaten the shifter community like none have done before.</i><br /><br />I loved the back stories we were treated to in this one. Finally we learn more about Jim, Derek, Curran, Roland, and Kate and I'm hungry to learn more. <b>The characters are getting fleshed out and the story is getting more complex without being overwhelming.</b> Andrews sticks to a select few of Kate's friends and acquaintances and really develops them and all I want to do is read more and more. This was the type of book where you're almost at the end and you're hoping 20 more pages will magically appear because you don't want it to stop. <br /><br />Kate has more than just grown on me at this point too; <b>I've got a full blown girl-crush on her now.</b> She's strong, funny, caring, snarky, and just a complete badass. I can't wait to read more of her adventures.<br /><br />I also like Curran more now since he's slowly progressed from the snarling caveman (cavelion?) from the first book. He's still decidedly alpha and scary, but not to the point where I'm afraid for Kate to be around him. He loves her and cares for her and he's sexy as hell. I honestly couldn't stop smiling after I read the last page and even after I closed the book I had a stupid grin on my face. <br /><br />This was a fantastic book and May can't come soon enough.<b> Ilona Andrews's books have moved on to my list of automatic buys</b> and if you liked this one as much as I did, check out <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/48999094" rel="nofollow noopener">On the Edge</a>, which was written after. It's a completely different series but the quality of Magic Strikes is also apparent in On the Edge as well.<br /><br />Check out my reviews of books two and four in this series: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45911879" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/60139860" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bleeds</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4652877282875403984" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

So many great moments. This book gets ALL THE STARS<br/><br/><b>Kate Daniels Buddy Read/Reread May 25 with the gang at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA)</a></b><br/><br/><b>Revised Fangirl Review upon the Re-read of the series before Magic Breaks is Released.</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/kateandcurran_zpsd4df0f38.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText9261742836546260216" style="display:none">Yes I'm reading the Kate Daniels Series AGAIN and guess what I love it a little more every time. 3rd read and this is still my favorite of the series. So many great moments. This book gets ALL THE STARS<br><br><b>Kate Daniels Buddy Read/Reread May 25 with the gang at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA)</a></b><br><br><b>Revised Fangirl Review upon the Re-read of the series before Magic Breaks is Released.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/kateandcurran_zpsd4df0f38.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Magic Strikes has <b>Gladiator style fighting with MAGIC</b> so it is even better, sexual tension so thick you can cut it with a knife, flying palaces in a separate realm and a murder mystery as good as any crime novel.<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/gladiator" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I loved it even more the second time around. All the quips, the intense and extremely entertaining battles, the budding relationship between Raphael and Andrea, the extreme sexual tension, Curran staking his claim on the ever reluctant Kate:<br><br><i>“Also, when he opened the door to leave, Curran told him very casually that if Jim wanted to pick fights with his future mate, he was welcome to do so, but he should keep in mind that Curran wouldn’t come and rescue him when you beat his ass. You should have seen Jim’s face.”<br>“His what?”<br><b>“His mate, M-A-T-E.”</b><br>I cursed.<br>Andrea grinned. “I thought that would make your day. And now you’re stuck with him in here for three days and you get to fight together in the Arena. It’s so romantic. Like a honeymoon.”</i><br><br>There are so many great moments in this, I loved so many characters. Saiman is slightly creepy with a god complex but turns out he is a quarter God so it is deserved. The shapeshifter equivalent to the Scooby-Doo gang, who pulls together to help Derrek, who has gotten in over his head in attempt to save a pretty girl. Kate’s background and her well-earned daddy issues come more to light in this as well as her reluctance to form attachments. Curran always a favorite proves just how far he is willing to go to save the woman he has decided is his.<br><br><i>”Have you ever seen a lion hunt a herd?”<br>“No.”<br>“They are very single-minded. When a loin stalks a herd, he sneaks in close, lies down, and surveys them to choose his victim. He takes his time. The deer or buffalo have no idea he’s near. <b>He finds his prey and then explodes from his hiding place and grabs it. Even if another, perfectly serviceable animal ends up within his reach, he isn’t going to alter his course. He has chosen, and he would rather go hungry than change his mind.”</b></i><br><br>Kate I don’t think you stand a chance. So much better the second time through and I loved every heart-thumping moment of it.<br><br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/castleintheair_zpsd46f2330.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404743933i/10277376._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo castleintheair_zpsd46f2330.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Initial Review 9/25/13</b><br><br>Kate Daniels once mercenary and now a semi-member of a Magical Order of Knights never seems to have small problems. She always has if you don’t succeed the world is all doomed problems. This book is no different there are some things that don’t seem all together human and an illegal fight ring going on in Atlanta. Derek is in trouble too and won’t tell Kate what is going on and Jim is hiding things from Curran as well. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Just reflecting on the fact that when the Universe punches you in the teeth, it never just lets you fall down. It kicks you in the ribs a couple of times and dumps mud on your head.”</i>
</b><br><br>It also seems that Kate has caught the eye of The Beast Lord who may be trying to court her using a few unusual methods involving food and a little breaking and entering. The tension between them is insane and I eat up every moment they are on the page together. I struggle between wanting them to get together and wanting to drag that moment out a little longer.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Go play your games with Jim. I'll find you both when I need you."<br>Arrogant asshole. "I tell you what, if you find us before those three days run out, I'll cook you a damn dinner and serve it to you naked."<br>"Is that a promise?"<br>"Yes…..”</i>
</b><br><br>There is the introduction of a few new characters Dali being one of my favorite new additions. She is a vegetarian Were-tiger that helps the team in the gladiator pit in an interesting and unusual way.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I do shodo magic,” Dali said. “I curse through calligraphy. I have to write the curse out on a piece of paper and I can’t move while I do it. One smudge, and I might kill the lot of us.”<br>Oh good.<br>“But don’t worry.” Dali waved her arms. “It’s so precise, it usually doesn’t work at all.”<br>Better and better.</i>
</b><br><br>Magic Bites was just ok, I liked Magic Burns more but I absolutely loved Magic Strikes. The story arc of the murder mystery, the illegal fighting pit, some more backstory into Kate’s upbringing, Saimion and all his weirdness and the building relationship of Kate and Curran kept me on the edge of my seat. I could not put this book down I literally finished it at 3 am and got up at 6 am to go to work <br><br>Well done a fantastic addition to the series and the strongest book so far. The first two books are well worth reading to get to this one. And again the last few pages be still my beating heart. It made me want to jump into the next book as soon as humanly possible. <br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9261742836546260216" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1156910548" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2374366803707580478"><b>First reread January 2015<br/><br/>Original rating: 5<br/>New rating: 10</b><br/><br/><i>☆☆☆ Post-Shift Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br/><b>Just Another Day in the Life of Kate Daniels</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422176678i/13467151.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>►<b>8.00 a.m.:</b> roll out of bed after getting 2 hours of sleep. Realize you're hungry. Open the fridge to get some of that leftover apple pie. <b>The plate is empty.</b> Strange.<br/>► <b>8.30 a.m.:</b> rescue your teenage werewolf sidekick from Saiman. Watch Saiman change form and <b>throw up in your mouth</b> a little. <br/>► <b>9.00 a.m.:</b> find out His Furriness became Beast Lord at the</span>
  <span id="freeText2374366803707580478" style="display:none"><b>First reread January 2015<br><br>Original rating: 5<br>New rating: 10</b><br><br><i>☆☆☆ Post-Shift Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br><b>Just Another Day in the Life of Kate Daniels</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422176678i/13467151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>►<b>8.00 a.m.:</b> roll out of bed after getting 2 hours of sleep. Realize you're hungry. Open the fridge to get some of that leftover apple pie. <b>The plate is empty.</b> Strange.<br>► <b>8.30 a.m.:</b> rescue your teenage werewolf sidekick from Saiman. Watch Saiman change form and <b>throw up in your mouth</b> a little. <br>► <b>9.00 a.m.:</b> find out His Furriness became Beast Lord at the tender age of 15 after chopping Andorf's head off. <b>This is going to be a long day.</b><br>► <b>9.30 a.m.:</b> your best friend tells you she doesn't want to be Raphael's TWT-IHFB. <b>Oh boy.</b><br>► <b>10.00 a.m.:</b> have a conversation with His Fussiness about <b>kissing his ass</b>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422183078i/13468319.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>10.30 a.m.:</b> hand Saiman a needle so he can <b>pop his head with it</b>. It's obscuring your view of the room.<br>► <b>11.00 a.m.:</b> listen to Jim telling you about a <b>weredingo</b>. Consider yourself lucky he didn't steal your baby.<br>► <b>11.30 a.m.:</b> try to smile. Aim for sweet. End up looking like a <b>psycho-killer</b>.<br>► <b>12.00 a.m.:</b> listen to a lecture about the different shapeshifter courtship customs. Aunt B. A cat on the ceiling. A fan. Mist. <b>That's boudas for you</b>.<br>► <b>12.30 a.m.:</b> go sightseeing with Jim. Visit a jungle and a flying palace. Play with the locals. <b>Chop a few arms off</b>. Things are looking up.<br>► <b>1.00 p.m.:</b> tell His Furriness he's a deadly psychopath with a god complex. Then tell him you're <b>having rough sex with Jim</b>. Bad idea.<br>► <b>1.30 p.m.:</b> temporary insanity. Oh. My. God. <b>The Universe just exploded</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422182147ra/13468218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>2.00 p.m.:</b> explain to your furry friends why you want Cesare's head. Then proceed to explain how you plan to <b>resurrect it and make it relive its death</b> over and over again. Did you just say all that out loud? Yep. You did. <br>► <b>2.30 p.m.:</b> the Beast Lord asks you <b>why you always attract creeps</b>. Ha! He walked right into that one, yes, he did.<br>► <b>3.00 p.m.:</b> Andrea says M-A-T-E. <b>You curse</b>. Then consider strangling her a little.<br>► <b>3.30 p.m.:</b> fight in the arena. Jim tells you to be sloppy. <b>You try</b>.<br>► <b>4.00 p.m.:</b> have a conversation about sausages with your furry friends. <i>
  <b>Die, die, die, die.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422181927ra/13468163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>4.30 p.m.:</b> Raphael hands you a fan in case you get hot. Curran doesn't think you need it. <b>This cat's such a bore</b>.<br>► <b>5.00 p.m.:</b> remember the good old days with daddy Voron back when you were thirteen. <b>Sightseeing in South America</b>. Visiting arenas. Slaughtering things a bit.<br>► <b>5.30 p.m.:</b> another fight in the arena. Blade-sprouting silver golem ✓ Troll (aka the overgrown log) ✓ Ancient vampire ✓ Enjoy seeing them die ✓ <b>This is so much fun</b>.<br>► <b>6.00 p.m.:</b> take a relaxing bath in a hot tub. <b>Try to pretend the Beast Lord isn't in there with you</b>. Oh. My. God. The Universe just exploded again.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422182147ra/13468218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>6.30 p.m.:</b> yet another fight in the arena. <b>Oh, look, it's the Scarlet Star</b>. <i>"Hessaad." Mine. "Ud." Die.</i> Sorry daddy, I think I just broke your sword.<br>► <b>7.00 p.m.:</b> Oh look, it's the flying palace again. <b>Feeling suddenly very tired</b>. It's been a long day.<br>► <b>7.30 p.m.:</b> Lose a little blood. <b>Cut a head off</b>. Feel much better.<br>► <b>8.00 p.m.:</b> find out cats are suicidal morons. <b>Who would have thought?</b><br>► <b>8.30 p.m.:</b> try telling the people in your head to shut up. <b>It doesn't work</b>. Oh look, a cat.<br>► <b>9.00 p.m.:</b> go home. Find someone in your kitchen. <b>Wait. What?</b> <br>► <b>9.30 p.m.:</b> read a note reminding you of an upcoming dinner. <b>You're allowed to wear a bra and panties</b>. Oh boy.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422119861i/13458929.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br>*********<br><b>Original review (June 2014):</b><br><br><b>How much better can this series get!?</b> I’m seriously being blown away by every new instalment here. KD = pure awesomeness. Fabulous, exciting, memorable, astounding, staggering, wonderful, impressive, breathtaking, and nothing short of downright amazing. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418726472ra/12883198.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Ever went on a roller coaster ride?</b> Take that feeling, multiply it by 10 and you might get an idea of what this book is like. There is so much to take here that my heart must have stopped beating quite a few times as I was <s>reading</s> devouring Magic Strikes. The world building blew me away (again). It's even richer and more complex than in previous instalments. I didn’t think it was possible but yes, the Andrews got even better at it! This series is probably the better-crafted I have ever read. We had to wait for the third book in the series to find out about Kate’s blood and why she is so special but it was handled very well by the authors. Situations and characters take time to evolve and develop within the series but it doesn’t feel forced as all things are revealed in due time. There is still a lot to figure out about Kate though which leaves room for much more development in instalments to come.<br><br>I think what I like most about this series is that it is so well-balanced. <b>The action and battle scenes are mind-blowing</b> (and that’s saying a lot since I usually hate battle scenes), there is emotion, lots of humour, mystery, mythology… Everything really! <br><br><b>Oh and the characters!</b> Kate &amp; Curran are just great (I love that the romance part of the book is only a subplot so far and not taking over the whole series), the Derek situation is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[heartbreaking <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, Saiman is a total creep but I love him, Julie &amp; Dali are both welcome additions to the cast of characters, I love Andrea, I love Raphael… As I said in a previous review I think I just love everything single character in this series, even the evil ones!<br><br><b>What else? The quotes! The quotes!</b> Sorry, I can't resist it.<blockquote>Seven pairs of glowing eyes stared at me: four green, three yellow. Judging by the glow, the shapeshifter crew hovered on the verge of going furry. One of their own was dead and they were out for blood. I kept my tone light. “You fellows ever thought of hiring out as a Christmas lights crew? You’d make a fortune.”</blockquote><blockquote>A shadow crossed Andrea’s face. “I don’t want to be his TWT-IHFB” “What does that mean?” “That Weird Thing I Haven’t Fucked Before.” I choked on a bite of gyro.</blockquote><blockquote>“His Majesty needs a can-I girl anyway. And I’m not it.” “A can-I girl?” Andrea frowned. I leaned back. “Can I fetch you your food, Your Majesty? Can I tell you how strong and mighty you are, Your Majesty? Can I pick out your fleas, Your Majesty? Can I kiss your ass, Your Majesty? Can I…” It dawned on me that Raphael was sitting very still. Frozen, like a statue, his gaze fixed on the point above my head. “He’s standing behind me, isn’t he?” Andrea nodded slowly. “Technically it should be “may I,” Curran said, his voice deeper than I remembered. “Since you’re asking permission.” Why me? “To answer your question, yes, you may kiss my ass. Normally I prefer to maintain my personal space, but you’re a Friend of the Pack and your services have proven useful once or twice. I strive to accommodate the wishes of persons friendly to my people. My only question is, would your kissing my ass be obeisance, grooming, or foreplay?”</blockquote><blockquote>Saiman sighed. “At the risk of sounding crude, wooing you is like playing basketball with a porcupine. No compliment goes unpunished.”</blockquote><blockquote>I gave him a smile. I was aiming for sweet, but he turned a shade paler and scooted a bit farther from me. Note to self: work more on sweet and less on psycho-killer.</blockquote><blockquote>Curran looked back at me. “Why is it you always attract creeps?”<br>“You tell me.” Ha! Walked right into that one, yes, he did.</blockquote><blockquote>As he passed me, he leaned to Curran and handed him a paper fan folded from some sort of flyer.<br>Curran looked at the fan. “What?”<br>“An emergency precaution, Your Majesty. In case the lady faints.”<br>Curran just stared at him.<br>Raphael strode toward the Pit, turned, flexed a bit, and winked at me.<br>“Give me that,” I told Curran. “I need to fan myself.”<br>“No, you don’t.”</blockquote><b>Get me the next instalment! Quick!</b><br><br>• <b>Book 1</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156913295" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 2</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1136556683" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 4</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1222662503" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bleeds</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 5</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156907200" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Slays</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 6</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1087380222" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Rises</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 7</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1222671908" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Breaks</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 8</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088122695" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Shifts</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 9</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1388386563" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Binds</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 10</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1767301739" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Triumphs</a> ★★★★<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405928334ra/10472755.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1211837098?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=paranormal-mystery">paranormal-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=werewolves-and-other-furry-shifters">werewolves-and-other-furry-shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1211837098" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17990568965167582262">If you haven't read this series yet, you need to at least read the first three. The first two books were good, but this one is magic! :)<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432606729ra/14987637.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Originally read in February of 2015. Rereading with the Ilona Andrews Addicts group.<br/><br/>Here's my original review:</i><br/><br/>Best one yet in the series! Have I mentioned how much I love Kate Daniels? Oh yeah, I guess I have, just in every other review of these books. She is so funny and sarcastic. I find myself chuckling while reading.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"What kind of shapeshifter has orange f</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17990568965167582262" style="display:none">If you haven't read this series yet, you need to at least read the first three. The first two books were good, but this one is magic! :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432606729ra/14987637.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Originally read in February of 2015. Rereading with the Ilona Andrews Addicts group.<br><br>Here's my original review:</i><br><br>Best one yet in the series! Have I mentioned how much I love Kate Daniels? Oh yeah, I guess I have, just in every other review of these books. She is so funny and sarcastic. I find myself chuckling while reading.<br><br><b>
  <i>"What kind of shapeshifter has orange fur anyway?"<br>"Weredingo."<br>Now I'd seen everything. Well, at least he didn't steal my baby.<br>...<br><br>I gave him a smile. I was aiming for sweet, but he turned a shade paler and scooted a bit farther from me. Note to self: work more on sweet and less on psycho-killer.</i>
</b><br><br>In this book, we get to experience the "Midnight Games", which remind me of some of the video games that my sons play , like League of Legends or TF2. They have gladiator-style fights in an arena one-on-one, but then there is a competition for team fighting for a big prize. Each team has seven members, and each member has to play a certain role. There is the Stone, the Swordsmaster, the Shield, the Shiv, the Spell, the Stratego, and the Sling. There is a lot of fighting and action, but with the usual humor mixed in.<br><br>It is also fun to watch Curran and Kate get closer. I like how there is no insta-love in these books at all. As a matter of fact, come on, already!! Sheesh!<br><br><b>
  <i>Curran looked back at me. "Why is it you always attract creeps?"<br>"You tell me." Ha! Walked right into that one, yes, he did. </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/burn" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424929651ra/13821091.gif" alt="burn photo: BURN BURN.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

The first was a gushing letter to the author. The second was a serious breakdown of the story and characters that just felt all wrong and the third was a half drunken, rambling poem modeled after “There once was a man from </span>
  <span id="freeText3012184129471323891" style="display:none">I promised myself that I would review this book after finishing it the second time around. I took expansive notes, I copied my favorite quotes down in preparation and I even went so far as to try to start writing a review while still reading. I made several attempts actually. The first was a gushing letter to the author. The second was a serious breakdown of the story and characters that just felt all wrong and the third was a half drunken, rambling poem modeled after “There once was a man from Nantucket”. What? I was on vacation. <br><br>I’d say it’s pretty obvious that all attempts failed miserably. You know what that means? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787864i/501350._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> this frigging book!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/596577.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> the murder mystery<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415358ra/819888.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> Curran’s pursuit of Kate<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415358i/819889.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> Kate’s badassery<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415358ra/819890.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> their non-stop taunting of each other<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415358ra/819891.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> the gladiator style battles<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415358ra/819892.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I even <b>LOVE</b> Saiman’s creep factor. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415358ra/819893.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><a href="http://litchickhitlist.blogspot.com/2013/07/magic-strikes-by-ilona-andrews.html" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1787582333" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1787582333" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1787582333?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=witches-wizards">witches-wizards</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=lions">lions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=minotaur">minotaur</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1787582333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2616578132228165320"><b>She should have seen this coming!</b><br/><br/>Kate has a number of things which occupy her mind and her life:<br/><br/><u>1.	The wellbeing of her new friends:</u><br/>-Jim betrays the pack, <br/>-Derek almost gets himself killed,<br/>-Raphael is crazy about Andrea and <br/>-Saiman has new scary enemies. They talk like human, smell like human, behave like human but what are they really? <br/>I am just happy that Kate has true friends finally.<br/><br/><u>2.	The dangers that her real family brings:</u><br/>We learn who her biological father is and what the consequences of </span>
  <span id="freeText2616578132228165320" style="display:none"><b>She should have seen this coming!</b><br /><br />Kate has a number of things which occupy her mind and her life:<br /><br /><u>1.	The wellbeing of her new friends:</u><br />-Jim betrays the pack, <br />-Derek almost gets himself killed,<br />-Raphael is crazy about Andrea and <br />-Saiman has new scary enemies. They talk like human, smell like human, behave like human but what are they really? <br />I am just happy that Kate has true friends finally.<br /><br /><u>2.	The dangers that her real family brings:</u><br />We learn who her biological father is and what the consequences of these revelations might be. <br />Okay, this will definitely make things more complex in the next books.<br /><br /><u>3.	The dangerous, illegal Midnight Games:</u><br />Full action, wonderful body conduct scenes in a primitive like arena. <br />The description of many, strangely magnificent, out of nightmare creatures that are battling together to prove who is the strongest. <br />For sure, the games in which Kate’s team participate were my favorites – especially the ones that they finish them off in less than a minute.<br /><br /><u>4.	Curran…</u><br />…more persistent than ever to have her:<br />Apparently, he has already decided that she is his mate. He just wants to have her firstly and answer her questions later. Certainly everybody else has realized his intentions except for Kate who does not understand the ways Alpha shifters play and the rules of courtship.<br />I really enjoy seeing them dancing around each other.<br /><br /><u>5.	Who has eaten her apple pie…</u><br />…or has Kate eaten it and she does not remember it?<br /> I cannot believe she was so careless and not paying attention to the details in this book. <br />Of course she should have seen it coming!<br /><br />At least the girl knows where she stands:<br /><i>"I can't let him kiss me again, because if he does, I'll sleep with him."</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="2616578132228165320" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1102238898" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17208335478022581386"><i> Reread 7/2018</i><br/><br/>I can't believe I didn't review this book back when I read it for the first time, this is definitely where the series began to pick up for me. This reread of the series has reminded me of why I like this series and this author. <br/><br/>Kate and Curran are the ultimate slow burn and that couple you find yourself shipping. I only made it to book 4 the first time around, and while I am taking a quick break after this one, I fully intend to finally catch up with this series. It's so good! It's</span>
  <span id="freeText17208335478022581386" style="display:none"><i> Reread 7/2018</i><br /><br />I can't believe I didn't review this book back when I read it for the first time, this is definitely where the series began to pick up for me. This reread of the series has reminded me of why I like this series and this author. <br /><br />Kate and Curran are the ultimate slow burn and that couple you find yourself shipping. I only made it to book 4 the first time around, and while I am taking a quick break after this one, I fully intend to finally catch up with this series. It's so good! It's reminded me of why I love PNR.<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------------<br />I don't feel like reviewing, so all I'll say is this book was awesome. This series is awesome and you should read it.<br />The end.</span>

<div id="review_198478924" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/198478924" />
    <a title="Lora" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4632071-lora"><img alt="Lora" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305237530p2/4632071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/198478924?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lora" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lora" href="/user/show/4632071-lora">Lora</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people on the same joy ride as me</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Lora by: </span>
      refer to first paragraph
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4632071-lora?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4632071-lora?shelf=series-still-follow">series-still-follow</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer198478924" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6448586188129153076"><b>I</b> can't believe no one mentioned this series to me, recommended this series to me, or spammed my profile with comments and PMs proclaiming this series' awesomeness. They should have. To everyone that didn't, you're on my shit list.<br/><br/><b>L</b>uckily for me, I <i>finally</i> made the decision on my own, like a big girl, and decided to give this series a try.<br/><b>O</b>nce I did, it wasn't exactly love at first page, but I've quickly moved into the honeymoon stage. Here's to the honeymoon never ending.<br/><b>V</b>ery rarely do I come a</span>
  <span id="freeText6448586188129153076" style="display:none"><b>I</b> can't believe no one mentioned this series to me, recommended this series to me, or spammed my profile with comments and PMs proclaiming this series' awesomeness. They should have. To everyone that didn't, you're on my shit list.<br /><br /><b>L</b>uckily for me, I <i>finally</i> made the decision on my own, like a big girl, and decided to give this series a try.<br /><b>O</b>nce I did, it wasn't exactly love at first page, but I've quickly moved into the honeymoon stage. Here's to the honeymoon never ending.<br /><b>V</b>ery rarely do I come across a series that I don't want to end, but the Kate Daniels series is one of those cases.<br /><b>E</b>very time I start one of these books, I know I won't be disappointed. This series has turned out one thousand times better than I ever imagined it would be.<br /><br /><b>T</b>his series takes time. The first book is good but not great, and it takes time getting used to the world as well as Kate's personality. It is more than worth it, though.<br /><b>H</b>aving not read a lot of UF titles prior to this series, I'm not claiming that my opinion on this genre is reputable. However, based on my meager experience with urban fantasy, I can honestly say that this series is the best <i>for me</i> in terms of characters, writing, pacing, and overall likability. (For a more reputable opinion on UF, please see Maja a.k.a. the Queen of Urban Fantasy's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4551536-maja" rel="nofollow noopener">profile</a>.)<br /><b>I</b> knew when we met Saiman in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38619.Magic_Bites__Kate_Daniels___1_" title="Magic Bites (Kate Daniels, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a> that he would eventually play a bigger role. And he definitely does in <i>Magic Strikes</i>. In this we find out more about his heritage, his original form, and we learn that there is more to him than just a lot of knowledge and a high sex drive. His character is very unique and refreshing.<br /><b>S</b>ome . . . *clears throat* . . . <i>progress</i> happens between Curran and Kate in this. I like the way their relationship is developing and the rate that it is doing so. Too many series seem to be too focused on the romance aspect too early on in the series. I like the way the authors have teased us thus far, only giving us little hints that there is much more than hostility boiling under the surface of their relationship.<br /><br /><b>S</b>eries like this don't come around for me that often. I've tried the first book in a lot of YA and adult series, and, even though there isn't anything necessarily wrong with them, they've failed to make me want to continue on and see what happens to the characters. A lot of series I've tried just don't seem worth the effort. But lately I've been gobbling up these books like Americans do turkey during Thanksgiving.<br /><b>E</b>arlier this year I was beginning to feel as if I was loosing my interest in reading. If you're a longtime book reader, you've probably been there. I have a back-up list, though: it is a list of books that I know can always pull me out of my reading slump, should I ever need them. This series will be added to that list.<br /><b>R</b>ight now Kate seems to have a lot of big things coming up in her life. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[e.g. meeting and killing Roland, admiting her true feelings to Curran, etc. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>I</b>'m very interested to see where things go and how some certain things play out.<br /><b>E</b>asy as it may seem to just let this series go and read one of the many other UF series out there, I think people should at least give this series a try. And just like with any book, there's going to be positive and negative opinions. I almost skipped this series entirely because of some of the negative reviews I've read, and to think how terrible that would've been! I've been having a blast with this series and I implore anyone with even an ounce of interest to go get <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38619.Magic_Bites__Kate_Daniels___1_" title="Magic Bites (Kate Daniels, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a> from their library and simply try it.<br /><b>S</b>eriously, go start reading this series now.<br /><b>!</b><br /><br />P.S. I thought chapter 15 was good, but that was before I read chapter 28. Yowzah.<br /><br />***********************************************<br /><br /><b>My reviews of other titles in this series:</b><br /><br />Book #1 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/194889805" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a><br />Book #2 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/197030282" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a><br />Book #4 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/200481479" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bleeds</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6448586188129153076" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Ginger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14097149-ginger"><img alt="Ginger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593449448p2/14097149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2646433583?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ginger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ginger" href="/user/show/14097149-ginger">Ginger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14097149-ginger?shelf=2019">2019</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2646433583" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15481472422777419671"><b>5 STARS!!</b><br/><br/>I’ve finally figured out what rates a <b>5 STAR</b> book from me.<br/><b>When I stay up all night to finish it and suffer the next day at work!</b><br/><br/>Wow, I’m so glad I stuck with this urban fantasy series. I really loved <b>Magic Strikes</b>! It was a fun, entertaining and addicting book to read.<br/><br/><b>Magic Strikes</b> is the 3rd book in the <i>Kate Daniels</i> series.<br/><i>Ilona Andrews</i> really brought her A game with this edition. The 1st two books in the series were okay but <b>Magic Strikes</b> took this series to a whole new level.<br/><br/>The book</span>
  <span id="freeText15481472422777419671" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS!!</b><br /><br />I’ve finally figured out what rates a <b>5 STAR</b> book from me.<br /><b>When I stay up all night to finish it and suffer the next day at work!</b><br /><br />Wow, I’m so glad I stuck with this urban fantasy series. I really loved <b>Magic Strikes</b>! It was a fun, entertaining and addicting book to read.<br /><br /><b>Magic Strikes</b> is the 3rd book in the <i>Kate Daniels</i> series.<br /><i>Ilona Andrews</i> really brought her A game with this edition. The 1st two books in the series were okay but <b>Magic Strikes</b> took this series to a whole new level.<br /><br />The book starts off with Kate’s shapeshifter friend Derek getting caught at Saiman’s home. Derek is trying to steal tickets from Saiman for the Midnight games. This is a fighting tournament that is by invitation only and it’s a tournament that fights to the death. Kate must figure out why Derek is involved in this and why he’s going against his alpha, Curran.<br /><br />Curran, the Lord of the Beasts has forbidden all shapeshifters to compete in this tournament. It’s a threat to the shapeshifting community and is punishable by death. Why would Derek get caught up in going against his alpha and possibly causing himself to die in the process?<br /><br />This is only the beginning of this awesome plot. It’s so complex and really takes the series forward in a great way.<br /><br />We have recurring characters in this from Derek, Jim, Julie to many more. If you’ve read the 1st two books of the series, you’ll know who some of these characters are.<br />I suggest you start at the beginning with book 1, <b>Magic Bites</b> to get the full affect of all the recurring characters. I don't think this should be read as a stand alone and I believe you will like this book even more!<br /><br />Yes, the 1st book is decent and I enjoyed it. It didn't blow me away but I'm so glad I stuck with the series.<br />It finally paid off! It’s so much better by this point!<br />It could be that I'm invested in the much loved characters at this point? But I think it’s more then that. Some of the plot questions of Kate and her past is answered in <b>Magic Strikes</b> and I can’t wait to see where this series is going to go!!<br /><br />Highly recommended to urban fantasy lovers. This series has been fun and this latest addition, <b>Magic Strikes</b> has made it one of my favorite urban fantasy series so far!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15481472422777419671" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5407996463650191090">Holy mother of cliffhangers, I hate it when they do that!!<br/><br/>Okay, you got me.
